	DROP TABLE IF EXISTS PLANDESP; 
	CREATE TABLE PLANDESP ( COD_OBRA character(6),MEDICAO character(6),DTA_MEDICA date,DESCRICAO character(60),VALOR numeric(19,2),DTA_DESPES date,OPERADOR character(10),DATATUAL date ) WITH (OIDS=FALSE);
INSERT INTO PLANDESP VALUES ('000001','000001','2004-02-27','Descricao de testes',150,00,'2003-03-27','Master','1899-12-30' );
	DROP TABLE IF EXISTS PLANIMPO; 
	CREATE TABLE PLANIMPO ( COD_OBRA character(6),MEDICAO character(6),DTA_MEDICA date,COD_IMPOST character(6),VALOR numeric(19,2),DTA_IMPOST date,OPERADOR character(10),DATATUAL date ) WITH (OIDS=FALSE);
INSERT INTO PLANIMPO VALUES ('000001','000001','2004-02-27','000004',0,00,'2003-12-30','Master','2004-02-27' );
	DROP TABLE IF EXISTS PLANMATE; 
	CREATE TABLE PLANMATE ( COD_OBRA character(6),MEDICAO character(6),COD_MATER character(6),QTDE numeric(6,0),PRECO_UNIT numeric(14,2),NUM_PEDIDO character(6),OPERADOR character(10),DATATUAL timestamp without time zone ) WITH (OIDS=FALSE);
	DROP TABLE IF EXISTS PLANNFS; 
	CREATE TABLE PLANNFS ( COD_OBRA character(6),MEDICAO character(6),DTA_MEDICA date,NUMERO character(15),VALOR numeric(19,2),DTA_NOTA date,OPERADOR character(10),DATATUAL date ) WITH (OIDS=FALSE);
	DROP TABLE IF EXISTS PLANOBRA; 
	CREATE TABLE PLANOBRA ( COD_OBRA character(6),MEDICAO character(6),DATA date,OPERADOR character(10),DATATUAL timestamp without time zone ) WITH (OIDS=FALSE);
	DROP TABLE IF EXISTS PLANRECE; 
	CREATE TABLE PLANRECE ( COD_OBRA character(6),MEDICAO character(6),DTA_MEDICA date,NUMCHEQUE character(15),NF character(50),VALOR numeric(19,2),OPERADOR character(10),DATATUAL date ) WITH (OIDS=FALSE);
	DROP TABLE IF EXISTS PLANSERV;
